namespace = ehof_travel
########################################################################################################
############################################## EHOF Travel #############################################
########################################################################################################
country_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.001
	title = "ehof_ehof"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_window"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		graphical_culture = root
		room = "ehof_room"
	}
	location = event_target:ehof_megastructure_system
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ehof_phase
				value = 1
			}
		}
		text = "ehof_travel.001_01_desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ehof_phase
				value = 2
			}
		}
		text = "ehof_travel.001_02_desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ehof_phase
				value = 3
			}
		}
		text = "ehof_travel.001_03_desc"
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = ehof_phase
				value = 4
			}
		}
		text = "ehof_travel.001_04_desc"
	}
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		log = ui_1
		# save ehof system as event target
		ehof_mega_system = yes
		ehof_giga_new_set_ehof_basic_travel_cost = yes
		set_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy
		# move all ships to ehof if ehof can activate
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			}
			ehof_move_fleet_to_ehof = yes
		}
	}
	###############################################################################################################
	# DESTINATIONS ################################################################################################
	###############################################################################################################
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_header"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
		}
		name = "ehof_header_01"
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_flag = ehof_travel_diplomacy
			country_event = {
				id = ehof_travel.001
			}
		}
	}
	# Wormhole Cohesive
	option = {
		name = "ehof_category_01"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			ehof_giga_new_option_basic_requirement = yes
		}
		allow = {
			ehof_giga_new_option_cost_requirements = yes
		}
		ehof_giga_new_energy_option_cost = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			ehof_dest_01 = yes
		}
	}
	# Random
	option = {
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			check_variable = {
				which = ehof_phase
				value <= 4
			}
		}
		allow = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ehof_phase
						value = 4
					}
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= @ehof_target_p4
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ehof_phase
						value = 3
					}
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= @ehof_target_p3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ehof_phase
						value = 2
					}
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= @ehof_target_p2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = ehof_phase
						value = 1
					}
				}
				resource_stockpile_compare = {
					resource = energy
					value >= @ehof_target_p1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 4
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				energy = @ehof_target_neg_p4
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 3
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				energy = @ehof_target_neg_p3
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 2
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				energy = @ehof_target_neg_p2
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 1
				}
			}
			add_resource = {
				energy = @ehof_target_neg_p1
			}
		}
		name = "ehof_category_00"
		hidden_effect = {
			ehof_dest_02 = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "ehof_category_06"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_big"
		trigger = {
			any_system = {
				ehof_giga_new_basic_travel_conditions = yes
				is_binary = yes
			}
			has_country_flag = ehof_can_activate
			OR = {
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 4
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = ehof_phase
					value = 3
				}
			}
		}

		graphical_culture = root

# Create a specific star
country_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.003
	title = "ehof_ehof"
	is_triggered_only = yes
	diplomatic = yes
	custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_window"
	picture_event_data = {
		portrait = root
		graphical_culture = root
		room = "ehof_room"
	}
	location = event_target:ehof_megastructure_system
	desc = "ehof_travel.001_04_desc"
	immediate = {
		log = ui_3
		ehof_mega_system = yes
		set_country_flag = ehof_wormhole_to_cohesive
	}
	# Spawn a birch system
	option = {
		name = "ehof_sm_blackhole"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"
		trigger = {
			has_ascension_perk = ap_vast_expanses
			NOT = {
				any_system = {
					or = {
						has_star_flag = giga_birch_core
						is_star_class = sc_birch
					}
				}
			}
		}
		allow = {
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = energy
				value >= @ehof_target_p4
			}
			resource_stockpile_compare = {
				resource = ehof_sr_negative_mass
				value >= 15000
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			energy = @ehof_target_neg_p4
		}
		add_resource = {
			ehof_sr_negative_mass = -15000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ehof_create_sc_birch
			set_country_flag = should_spawn_covesive_@root
			country_event = {
				id = ehof_megastructure.500
			}
		}
	}
	# Spawn a QSO system
	option = {
		name = "ehof_sm_quasar"
		custom_gui = "ehof_mainui_option_small"

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = no
	force_open = yes
	title = ehof_travel.1001.NAME
	desc = ehof_travel.1001.DESC

	}

		name = ehof_travel.1001.a
	}
}
# A ship has surveyed a planet.
# Scope = Ship
# From = Planet
ship_event = {
	id = ehof_travel.1002
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hide_window = no
	force_open = yes
	title = ehof_travel.1002.NAME
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_1
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.1.DESC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_2
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.2.DESC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_3
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.3.DESC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_4
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.4.DESC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_5
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.5.DESC
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_6
			}
		}
		text = ehof_travel.1002.6.DESC
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_1
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_toxic
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_2
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_shattered_planet
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_3
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_frozen
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_4
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_molten
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_5
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_gas_giant
	}
	picture = {
		trigger = {
			from = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_6
			}
		}
		picture = GFX_evt_star_neutron
	}
	show_sound = event_scanner

	trigger = {
		from = {
			solar_system = {
				has_star_flag = ehof_system_created_by_@root.owner
			}
			OR = {
				has_planet_flag = code_world_1
				has_planet_flag = code_world_2
				has_planet_flag = code_world_3
				has_planet_flag = code_world_4
				has_planet_flag = code_world_5
				has_planet_flag = code_world_6
			}
		}
	}


	immediate = {
	}
	option = {
		name = ehof_travel.1002.a
	}
}

namespace = ehof_giga_new_rc
system_event = {
	id = ehof_giga_new_rc.0
	hide_window = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		from = { has_country_flag = ehof_spawn_reality_code }
		OR = {
			from = { ehof_giga_new_star_based_reality_code_spawn_flag = yes }
			AND = {
				from = {
					ehof_giga_new_planetary_reality_code_spawn_flag = yes
				}
				any_system_planet = {
					ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		from = {
			switch = {
				trigger = has_country_flag 
				ehof_code_toxic_world = {
					prev = {
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = {
								ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
							}

							ehof_giga_new_set_first_reality_code_arch = yes
						}
					}
				}
				ehof_code_broken_world = {
					prev = {
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = {
								ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
							}

							ehof_giga_new_set_second_reality_code_arch = yes
						}
					}
				}
				ehof_code_frozen_world = {
					prev = {
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = {
								ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
							}

							ehof_giga_new_set_third_reality_code_arch = yes
						}
					}
				}
				ehof_code_molten_world = {
					prev = {
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = {
								ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
							}

							ehof_giga_new_set_fourth_reality_code_arch = yes
						}
					}
				}
				ehof_code_gas_giant_world = {
					prev = {
						random_system_planet = {
							limit = {
								ehof_giga_new_planet_can_support_reality_code = yes
							}

							ehof_giga_new_set_fifth_reality_code_arch = yes
						}
					}
				}
				ehof_code_star_world = {
					ehof_giga_new_set_sixth_reality_code_arch = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
